\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Fortran API functions for MMG2D library. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Cecile Dobrzynski (Bx INP/\+Inria/\+UBordeaux) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
5 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
07 2015 
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
GNU Lesser General Public License. 
\end{DoxyCopyright}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Please, refer to the mmg2d/liblibmmg2d\+\_\+private.\+h file for functions documentation.
\end{DoxyNote}
Define the Fortran API functions for MMG2D library\+: adds function definitions with upcase, underscore and double underscore to match any fortran compiler. 

Definition in file \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functionsf__2d_8c_source}{API\+\_\+functionsf\+\_\+2d.\+c}}.
